add_namespace = legation_cities_green_gang_events

country_event = { # Intro (Used in intro screen as well. DO NOT DELETE!)
	id = legation_cities_events.1
	title = legation_cities_events.1.t
	desc = legation_cities_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_LEC_shanghai_river

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.1 option legation_cities_events.1.a"
		name = legation_cities_events.1.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes }
				country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.2 days = 3 }
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { LEC_is_legation_council_observer = yes }
				country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.3 days = 3 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.LEC_council_members
				if = {
					limit = { LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes }
					country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.2 days = 3 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.3 days = 3 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # We can vote
	id = legation_cities_events.2
	title = legation_cities_events.2.t

	desc = {
		text = legation_cities_events.2.d.germany
		trigger = { tag = GER }
	}
	desc = {
		text = legation_cities_events.2.d.japan
		trigger = { tag = JAP }
	}
	desc = {
		text = legation_cities_events.2.d.usa
		trigger = { tag = USA }
	}
	desc = {
		text = legation_cities_events.2.d.austria
		trigger = { tag = AUS }
	}
	desc = {
		text = legation_cities_events.2.d.belgium
		trigger = { tag = BEL }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_LEC_shanghai_river

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.2 option legation_cities_events.2.a"
		name = legation_cities_events.2.a
		trigger = { tag = USA }
		add_political_power = 25
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.2 option legation_cities_events.2.b"
		name = legation_cities_events.2.b
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = USA } }
		add_political_power = 25
	}
}

country_event = { #A Legation Navy?
	id = legation_cities_events.4
	title = legation_cities_events.4.t
	desc = legation_cities_events.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_battleship_kongo

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#Of course!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.4 option legation_cities_events.4.a"
		name = legation_cities_events.4.a
		set_global_flag = LEC_legation_navy_vote
		activate_mission = LEC_vote_timer
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes }
				country_event = legation_cities_events.5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { LEC_vote_delay = 2 }
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.LEC_council_members
				if = {
					limit = { LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes }
					country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.5 days = LEC_vote_delay }
					add_to_temp_variable = { LEC_vote_delay = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = legation_cities_events.5
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Legation navy? - voting
	id = legation_cities_events.5
	title = legation_cities_events.5.t
	desc = legation_cities_events.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_battleship_kongo

	trigger = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Let's see how this goes...
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.5 option legation_cities_events.observer"
		name = legation_cities_events.observer
		trigger = {
			LEC_has_legation_council_vote = no
		}
	}

	option = { #Yes
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.5 option legation_cities_events.vote_yes"
		name = legation_cities_events.vote_yes
		trigger = {
			LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_war = no
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#No
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.5 option legation_cities_events.vote_no"
		name = legation_cities_events.vote_no
		trigger = {
			LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.legations_no_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#Abstain
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.5 option legation_cities_events.vote_abstain"
		name = legation_cities_events.vote_abstain
		trigger = {
			LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 25
				tag = AUS
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.legations_abstain_votes = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Legation navy? - Result
	id = legation_cities_events.6
	title = legation_cities_events.6.t
	desc = legation_cities_events.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_battleship_kongo

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#Approved!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.6 option legation_cities_events.6.a"
		name = legation_cities_events.6.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				LEC_vote_passes = yes
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_AUTDEM_GER }
						has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_AUTDEM_JAP }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { LEC_currency_change = -1 }
		LEC_change_currency_reserves = yes
		country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.8 days = 30 }
		set_country_flag = LEC_navy_approved
	}

	option = {	#Denied!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.6 option legation_cities_events.6.b"
		name = legation_cities_events.6.b
		trigger = {
			LEC_vote_passes = no
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_AUTDEM_GER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_AUTDEM_JAP }
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -75
	}
}

country_event = { #Black Monday arrives
	id = legation_cities_events.7
	title = legation_cities_events.7.t
	desc = legation_cities_events.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NOR_black_monday

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#Argh
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.7 option legation_cities_events.7.a"
		name = legation_cities_events.7.a
		add_stability = -0.2
		custom_effect_tooltip = LEC_black_monday_tt
		set_temp_variable = { LEC_currency_change = -2 }
		LEC_change_currency_reserves = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_ideas = LEC_black_monday
	}
}

country_event = { #1936 Budget Finalized
	id = legation_cities_events.9
	title = legation_cities_events.9.t
	desc = legation_cities_events.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#I like money ngl
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.9 option legation_cities_events.9.a"
		name = legation_cities_events.9.a
		add_political_power = 25
		LEC_change_currency_reserves = yes
		activate_mission = LEC_budget_motion
		hidden_effect = {
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = LEC_budget_motion
				days = -60
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Vote on Russian Vote Restoration?
	id = legation_cities_events.10
	title = legation_cities_events.10.t
	desc = legation_cities_events.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#Of course!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.10 option legation_cities_events.10.a"
		name = legation_cities_events.10.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		set_global_flag = LEC_russia_vote
		activate_mission = LEC_vote_timer
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
				country_event = legation_cities_events.11
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { LEC_vote_delay = 2 }
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.LEC_council_members
				if = {
					limit = { LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes }
					country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.11 days = LEC_vote_delay }
					add_to_temp_variable = { LEC_vote_delay = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = legation_cities_events.11
				}
			}
		}
		var:global.russia = { country_event = legation_cities_events.12 }
	}

	option = {	#We don't need a vote...
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.10 option legation_cities_events.10.b"
		name = legation_cities_events.10.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_political_power = -50
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
			country_event = legation_cities_events.14
		}
		var:global.russia = { country_event = legation_cities_events.15 }
	}
}

				type = coastal_bunker
				level = 1
				province = {
					all_provinces = yes
					limit_to_border = no
					level > 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	# Disgree
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.34 option legation_cities_events.34.b"
		name = legation_cities_events.34.b
		army_experience = -5
		add_command_power = -20
	}
}

					limit = { LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes }
					country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.46 days = LEC_vote_delay }
					add_to_temp_variable = { LEC_vote_delay = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = legation_cities_events.46
				}
			}
		}
	}

		has_idea = LEC_currency_1
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#ok very good
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.60 option legation_cities_events.60.a"
		name = legation_cities_events.60.a
		#LEC will not collapse if a specific game rule has been set
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_AUTDEM_GER } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_AUTDEM_JAP } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { LEC_currency_change = 4 }
			LEC_change_currency_reserves = yes
		}
		else = {
			activate_mission = LEC_bankruptcy_warning
		}
	}
}

		add_war_support = -0.45
		set_global_flag = LEC_bankrupt

		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes
				NOT = { tag = GER }
				NOT = { tag = GEA }

			}
			LEC_remove_from_legation_council = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
			peace_out_non_neighbours_after_leaving_faction = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_legation_cities_open_door }
			remove_ideas = LEC_legation_cities_open_door
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = legation_cities_news_events.1
			GEA = { country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.72 days = 5 } }
			JAP = { country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.73 days = 5 } }

	}

country_event = { #Shanghai in Chaos - LEC
	id = legation_cities_events.74
	title = legation_cities_events.74.t
	desc = legation_cities_events.74.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_barricade

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_stability = 0.3
			country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.148 days = 365 }
		}
	}

	option = {	#The Germans won
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.74 option legation_cities_events.74.a"
		name = legation_cities_events.74.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				has_country_flag = GER_aggressive
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = GER_defensive
					has_country_flag = JAP_defensive
				}
			}
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = { has_trait = LEC_japanese_commander }
			retire = yes
		}
		GER = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = LEC
				autonomy_state = default_puppet
				end_wars = no
			}
		}
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:paternal_autocrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_popularities = {
				totalist = 0
				syndicalist = 0
				radical_socialist = 1
				social_democrat = 6
				social_liberal = 14
				market_liberal = 7
				social_conservative = 10
				authoritarian_democrat = 27
				paternal_autocrat = 23
				national_populist = 12
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_supply_lines_idea }
			remove_ideas = LEC_supply_lines_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_TMKKD_idea }
			remove_ideas = LEC_TMKKD_idea
		}
		GER = { country_event = legation_cities_events.75 }
		GEA = { country_event = legation_cities_events.75 }
		JAP = { country_event = legation_cities_events.76 }
	}
	option = {	#The Japanese won
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.74 option legation_cities_events.74.b"
		name = legation_cities_events.74.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				has_country_flag = JAP_aggressive
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = GER_defensive
					has_country_flag = JAP_defensive
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_war_with = JAP }
			force_capitulate = yes
		}
		else = {
			every_character = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = LEC_german_commander
						has_trait = LEC_british_commander
						has_trait = LEC_international_commander
					}
				}
				retire = yes
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = LEC
				autonomy_state = default_puppet
				end_wars = no
			}
		}
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_popularities = {
				totalist = 0
				syndicalist = 0
				radical_socialist = 1
				social_democrat = 6
				social_liberal = 14
				market_liberal = 9
				social_conservative = 8
				authoritarian_democrat = 27
				paternal_autocrat = 12
				national_populist = 23
			}
		}
		JAP = { country_event = legation_cities_events.75 }
		GEA = { country_event = legation_cities_events.76 }
		GER = { country_event = legation_cities_events.76 }
	}
}

		activate_mission = LEC_remove_germany_motion
	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.81 option legation_cities_events.81.b"
		name = legation_cities_events.81.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				add = party_popularity_100@national_populist
			}
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = { has_trait = LEC_german_commander }
			retire = yes
		}
		GER = { country_event = legation_cities_events.82 }
		GEA = { country_event = legation_cities_events.89 }

			limit = {
				is_chinese_tag = yes
				LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.88 days = 1 }
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes
				has_guaranteed = LEC
				NOT = { tag = GER }
			}
			country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.83 days = 1 }
		}

		}

				}
				add_popularity = {

			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = JAP }
			LEC = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = national_populist
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = national_populist
					popularity = 0.2
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = AST
					tag = CAN
					tag = GBR
				}
			}
			LEC = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_conservative
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 0.2
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			LEC = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = market_liberal
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = market_liberal

				}
			}
		}
	}

		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		lec_british_rise = yes
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
			country_event = legation_cities_events.103
		}
	}
	option = { #Just give up to the Chinese
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.101 option legation_cities_events.101.c"
		name = legation_cities_events.101.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { owns_state = 613 }
			var:613.owner = { is_chinese_tag = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = LEC_surrender_to_china
		set_global_flag = LEC_surrendered_to_china
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
				country_event = legation_cities_events.106
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { LEC_is_dismantled = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { var:613.owner = { is_chinese_tag = yes } }
			var:613.owner = { country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.104 days = 1 } }
		}
		else = {
			set_global_flag = LEC_bankrupt
			set_cosmetic_tag = LEC_shanghai
			remove_ideas = {
				LEC_currency_1
				LEC_currency_2
				LEC_currency_3
				LEC_currency_4
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#We are China now!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.101 option legation_cities_events.131.f"
		name = legation_cities_events.131.f
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 613
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1000 }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		lec_chinese_rise = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Legation Cities gets concessions
	id = legation_cities_events.127
	title = legation_cities_events.127.t
	desc = legation_cities_events.127.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		any_owned_state = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = LEC
				is_possible_legation_cities_state = yes
			}
			is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { tag = JAP } }
				NOT = { has_variable = ambition_area_@ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	# yes
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.127 option legation_cities_events.127.a"
		name = legation_cities_events.127.a
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LEC }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				OR = {
					is_core_of = LEC
					is_possible_legation_cities_state = yes
					AND = {
						is_core_china = yes
						LEC = { has_cosmetic_tag = LEC_china }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { tag = JAP } }
					NOT = { has_variable = ambition_area_@ROOT }
				}
			}
			remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes
			transfer_state_to = LEC
		}
		LEC = { country_event = legation_cities_events.128 }
	}
	option = {	# no
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.127 option legation_cities_events.127.b"
		name = legation_cities_events.127.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_political_power = -25
		LEC = {
			country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.129 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -0.5
		}
	}
	option = {	#Now we're screwed
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.130 option legation_cities_events.130.b"
		name = legation_cities_events.130.b
		trigger = {
			has_government = national_populist
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.1
		set_temp_variable = { LEC_currency_change = -1 }
		LEC_change_currency_reserves = yes
		country_event = { id = legation_cities_events.131 days = 5 }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -0.5
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_supply_lines_idea }
			remove_ideas = LEC_supply_lines_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_TMKKD_idea }
			remove_ideas = LEC_TMKKD_idea
		}
	}
	option = {	#Serves them right!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.130 option legation_cities_events.130.c"
		name = legation_cities_events.130.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = paternal_autocrat
		}
		add_political_power = 5
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -1
		}
	}
}

			}

				add_idea = LEC_volunteer_force
			}

			swap_ideas = {
				add_idea = LEC_volunteer_force
				remove_idea = LEC_volunteer_force_expanded

			limit = { has_completed_focus = LEC_expanding_the_volunteers }
			uncomplete_national_focus = { focus = LEC_expanding_the_volunteers uncomplete_children = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = LEC_establish_chinese_militia } }
			complete_national_focus = LEC_establish_chinese_militia
		}
	}
	option = {	#don't abolish it
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_events.143 option legation_cities_events.143.b"

country_event = { #Bailout the DAB?
	id = legation_cities_business_events.2
	title = legation_cities_business_events.2.t
	desc = legation_cities_business_events.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NOR_black_monday

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#Of course!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_business_events.2 option legation_cities_business_events.2.a"
		name = legation_cities_business_events.2.a
		set_global_flag = LEC_DAB_bailout_question
		activate_mission = LEC_vote_timer
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
				country_event = legation_cities_business_events.3
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { LEC_vote_delay = 2 }
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.LEC_council_members
				if = {
					limit = { LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes }
					country_event = { id = legation_cities_business_events.3 days = LEC_vote_delay }
					add_to_temp_variable = { LEC_vote_delay = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = legation_cities_business_events.3
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Bailout the DAB? - voting
	id = legation_cities_business_events.3
	title = legation_cities_business_events.3.t
	desc = legation_cities_business_events.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NOR_black_monday_2

	trigger = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Let's see how this goes...
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_business_events.3 option legation_cities_events.observer"
		name = legation_cities_events.observer
		trigger = {
			LEC_has_legation_council_vote = no
		}
	}

	option = { #Yes
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_business_events.3 option legation_cities_events.vote_yes"
		name = legation_cities_events.vote_yes
		trigger = {
			LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				OR = {
					tag = BEL
					is_american_tag = yes
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#No
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_business_events.3 option legation_cities_events.vote_no"
		name = legation_cities_events.vote_no
		trigger = {
			LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = GER
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.legations_no_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#Abstain
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_business_events.3 option legation_cities_events.vote_abstain"
		name = legation_cities_events.vote_abstain
		trigger = {
			LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = JAP
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 25
				tag = AUS
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.legations_abstain_votes = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Bailout the DAB? - Result
	id = legation_cities_business_events.4
	title = legation_cities_business_events.4.t
	desc = legation_cities_business_events.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NOR_black_monday_2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#Approved!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_business_events.4 option legation_cities_business_events.4.a"
		name = legation_cities_business_events.4.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				LEC_vote_passes = yes
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_AUTDEM_GER }
						has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_AUTDEM_JAP }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { LEC_currency_change = -1 }
		LEC_change_currency_reserves = yes
		country_event = { id = legation_cities_business_events.6 days = 4 }
	}
	option = {	#Denied!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_business_events.4 option legation_cities_business_events.4.b"
		name = legation_cities_business_events.4.b
		trigger = {
			LEC_vote_passes = no
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_AUTDEM_GER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_AUTDEM_JAP }
				}
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				country_event = { id = legation_cities_business_events.5 days = 7 }
			}
			50 = {
				country_event = { id = legation_cities_business_events.6 days = 7 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #British businessmen think Shanghai is receiving too much investment
	id = legation_cities_british_events.1
	title = legation_cities_british_events.1.t
	desc = legation_cities_british_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NOR_black_monday

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owns_state = 326 #Hong Kong
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = LEC_ongoing_storyline
	}

	option = {	#What if we put money into Hong Kong?
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_british_events.1 option legation_cities_british_events.1.a"
		name = legation_cities_british_events.1.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { LEC_currency_reserves > 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = LEC_currency_reserves
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_SOCCON }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { LEC_currency_change = -1 }
		LEC_change_currency_reserves = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = legation_cities_british_events.2 days = 10 }
			country_event = { id = legation_cities_british_events.3 days = 20 }
		}
	}
	option = {	#Ignore them
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_british_events.1 option legation_cities_british_events.1.b"
		name = legation_cities_british_events.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_AUTDEM_GER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_AUTDEM_JAP }
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_NATPOP }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = legation_cities_british_events.4 days = 10 }
			country_event = { id = legation_cities_british_events.5 days = 20 }
		}
	}
	option = {	#Cancel the plans
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_british_events.1 option legation_cities_british_events.1.c"
		name = legation_cities_british_events.1.c
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { LEC_currency_reserves < 9 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { LEC_currency_temp = 10 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { LEC_currency_temp = LEC_currency_reserves }
				factor = LEC_currency_temp
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_AUTDEM_GER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_AUTDEM_JAP }
				}
			}
		}
		LEC_change_currency_reserves = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:LEC_has_british_vote = {
				country_event = { id = legation_cities_british_events.12 days = 10 }
			}
			country_event = { id = legation_cities_british_events.6 days = 10 }
			country_event = { id = legation_cities_british_events.7 days = 20 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Australia goes syndie/AFM and loses their China stuff
	id = legation_cities_british_events.28
	title = legation_cities_british_events.28.t
	desc = legation_cities_british_events.28.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_LEC_shanghai_river

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = LEC
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = AST_hong_kong
			LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				GBR = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			}
			GBR = { save_global_event_target_as = LEC_has_british_vote }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				CAN = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			}
			CAN = { save_global_event_target_as = LEC_has_british_vote }
		}
		else = {
			clear_global_event_target = LEC_has_british_vote
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_british_events.28 option legation_cities_british_events.28.a"
		name = legation_cities_british_events.28.a
		trigger = { has_event_target = LEC_has_british_vote }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = AST_hong_kong }
			clr_country_flag = AST_hong_kong
			event_target:LEC_has_british_vote = { set_country_flag = AST_hong_kong }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes }
			save_event_target_as = LEC_AST_had_vote
		}
		LEC_remove_from_legation_council = yes
		LEC = { country_event = legation_cities_british_events.26 }
		event_target:LEC_has_british_vote = { country_event = legation_cities_british_events.29 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_british_events.28 option legation_cities_british_events.28.a"
		name = legation_cities_british_events.28.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_event_target = LEC_has_british_vote } }
		clr_country_flag = AST_hong_kong
		LEC_remove_from_legation_council = yes
		LEC = { country_event = legation_cities_british_events.26 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Vote on British Vote Restoration?
	id = legation_cities_british_events.41
	title = legation_cities_british_events.41.t
	desc = legation_cities_british_events.41.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#Of course!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_british_events.41 option legation_cities_british_events.41.a"
		name = legation_cities_british_events.41.a
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		activate_mission = LEC_vote_timer
		set_global_flag = LEC_britain_vote
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
				country_event = legation_cities_british_events.42
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { LEC_vote_delay = 2 }
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.LEC_council_members
				if = {
					limit = { LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes }
					country_event = { id = legation_cities_british_events.42 days = LEC_vote_delay }
					add_to_temp_variable = { LEC_vote_delay = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = legation_cities_british_events.42
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:LEC_has_british_vote = { country_event = legation_cities_british_events.43 }
	}
	option = {	#We don't need a vote...
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_british_events.41 option legation_cities_british_events.41.b"
		name = legation_cities_british_events.41.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = party_popularity_100@social_conservative
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_SOCCON }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = LEC_brits_vote
		add_political_power = -100
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes
				NOT = { tag = event_target:LEC_has_british_vote }
			}
			country_event = legation_cities_british_events.45
		}
		event_target:LEC_has_british_vote = { country_event = legation_cities_british_events.46 }
	}
}

		}

				tag = AUS
			}
		}

	}

				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
				country_event = { id = legation_cities_american_events.14 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = LEC_new_high_commissioner
		lec_american_rise = yes
	}
	option = {	#Jap time baby
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_american_events.13 option legation_cities_american_events.13.b"
		name = legation_cities_american_events.13.b
		trigger = {
			JAP = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
			OR = {
				national_populist > 0.18
				has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_NATPOP }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0.9
			modifier = {
				add = party_popularity_100@national_populist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
				country_event = { id = legation_cities_american_events.15 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = LEC_new_high_commissioner
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = national_populist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		lec_japanese_rise = yes
	}
	option = {	#Krauts it is
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_american_events.13 option legation_cities_american_events.13.c"
		name = legation_cities_american_events.13.c
		trigger = {
			GER = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
			OR = {
				paternal_autocrat > 0.18
				has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_NATPOP }
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
				country_event = { id = legation_cities_american_events.16 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = LEC_new_high_commissioner
		every_character = {
			limit = { has_trait = LEC_japanese_commander }
			retire = yes
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		lec_german_rise = yes
	}
	option = {	#Anglos
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_american_events.13 option legation_cities_american_events.13.e"
		name = legation_cities_american_events.13.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				CAN = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
				AST = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = LEC_AST_governor
					social_conservative > 0.18
				}
				has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_SOCCON }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1.1
			modifier = {
				add = party_popularity_100@social_conservative
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_NATPOP }
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_MARLIB }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
				country_event = { id = legation_cities_american_events.17 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = LEC_new_high_commissioner

			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = no
		}

		}

	}

country_event = { #Vote on American Vote Restoration?
	id = legation_cities_american_events.23
	title = legation_cities_american_events.23.t
	desc = legation_cities_american_events.23.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#Of course!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_american_events.23 option legation_cities_american_events.23.a"
		name = legation_cities_american_events.23.a
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		set_global_flag = LEC_america_vote
		activate_mission = LEC_vote_timer
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
				country_event = legation_cities_american_events.24
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { LEC_vote_delay = 2 }
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.LEC_council_members
				if = {
					limit = { LEC_has_legation_council_vote = yes }
					country_event = { id = legation_cities_american_events.24 days = LEC_vote_delay }
					add_to_temp_variable = { LEC_vote_delay = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = legation_cities_american_events.24
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			save_global_event_target_as = LEC_has_american_vote
			country_event = legation_cities_american_events.25
		}
	}

	option = {	#Do it ourselves!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_american_events.23 option legation_cities_american_events.23.b"
		name = legation_cities_american_events.23.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = party_popularity_100@market_liberal
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
			country_event = legation_cities_american_events.29
		}
		FROM = { country_event = legation_cities_american_events.30 }
	}

	option = {	#Get out of here, Yanks, we're biased now
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_american_events.23 option legation_cities_american_events.23.c"
		name = legation_cities_american_events.23.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes }
			country_event = legation_cities_american_events.31
		}
		FROM = { country_event = legation_cities_american_events.32 }
	}
}

					has_war_with = NEE
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15

					tag = ENT
					tag = AST
					tag = BEL
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes = 1 }
	}

		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				tag = GER
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				tag = JAP
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.legations_no_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#Abstain
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_american_events.24 option legation_cities_events.vote_abstain"
		name = legation_cities_events.vote_abstain

			modifier = {
				factor = 25
				tag = AUS
			}
		}

	}
}

country_event = { #The Japanese trying to obtain influence in Tianjin: terrorist attack time
	id = legation_cities_japanese_events.1
	title = legation_cities_japanese_events.1.t
	desc = legation_cities_japanese_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NOR_black_monday

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	# Agree
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_japanese_events.1 option legation_cities_japanese_events.1.a"
		name = legation_cities_japanese_events.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -20
		lec_japanese_rise = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = { country_event = { id = legation_cities_japanese_events.18 days = 2 } }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					LEC_is_legation_council_member = yes
					NOT = { tag = JAP }
				}
				country_event = { id = legation_cities_japanese_events.19 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	# Refuse
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event legation_cities_japanese_events.1 option legation_cities_japanese_events.1.b"
		name = legation_cities_japanese_events.1.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = national_populist }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = LEC_path option = LEC_PATH_NATPOP }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				country_event = { id = legation_cities_japanese_events.20 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}
